- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-882">Bessere Leistung beim Abrufen von Ressourcen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-882">Better performance when retrieving resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-883">Siehe [Verpacken und Bereitstellen von Ressourcen](../../../docs/framework/resources/packaging-and-deploying-resources-in-desktop-apps.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-883">See [Packaging and Deploying Resources](../../../docs/framework/resources/packaging-and-deploying-resources-in-desktop-apps.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-884">Verbesserte ZIP-Komprimierung zur Reduzierung der Größe einer komprimierten Datei.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-884">Zip compression improvements to reduce the size of a compressed file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-885">Siehe <xref:System.IO.Compression?displayProperty=nameWithType>-Namespace.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-885">See the <xref:System.IO.Compression?displayProperty=nameWithType> namespace.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-886">Anpassen von Reflektionskontext zum Überschreiben des Standardreflektionsverhaltens mit der <xref:System.Reflection.Context.CustomReflectionContext>-Klasse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-886">Ability to customize a reflection context to override default reflection behavior through the <xref:System.Reflection.Context.CustomReflectionContext> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-887">Unterstützung der Version 2008 des IDNA-Standards (Internationalized Domain Names in Applications) beim Verwenden der <xref:System.Globalization.IdnMapping?displayProperty=nameWithType>-Klasse in [!INCLUDE[win8](../../../includes/win8-md.md)].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-887">Support for the 2008 version of the Internationalized Domain Names in Applications (IDNA) standard when the <xref:System.Globalization.IdnMapping?displayProperty=nameWithType> class is used  on [!INCLUDE[win8](../../../includes/win8-md.md)].</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-888">Delegieren des Zeichenfolgenvergleichs an das Betriebssystem, wobei Unicode 6.0 implementiert wird, wenn .NET Framework in [!INCLUDE[win8](../../../includes/win8-md.md)] verwendet wird.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-888">Delegation of string comparison to the operating system, which implements Unicode 6.0, when the .NET Framework is used on [!INCLUDE[win8](../../../includes/win8-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-889">Bei Ausführung auf anderen Plattformen verwendet .NET Framework eigene Zeichenfolgenvergleichsdaten, wobei Unicode 5.x. implementiert wird.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-889">When running on other platforms, the .NET Framework includes its own string comparison data, which implements Unicode 5.x.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-890">Siehe <xref:System.String>-Klasse und den Abschnitt "Hinweise" der <xref:System.Globalization.SortVersion>-Klasse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-890">See the <xref:System.String> class and the Remarks section of the <xref:System.Globalization.SortVersion> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-891">Berechnen der Hashcodes für Zeichenfolgen pro Anwendungsdomäne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-891">Ability to compute the hash codes for strings on a per application domain basis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-892">Siehe [\<UseRandomizedStringHashAlgorithm>-Element](../../../docs/framework/configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/userandomizedstringhashalgorithm-element.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-892">See [\<UseRandomizedStringHashAlgorithm> Element](../../../docs/framework/configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/userandomizedstringhashalgorithm-element.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-893">Typspiegelung unterstützt eine Teilung zwischen <xref:System.Type> und <xref:System.Reflection.TypeInfo>-Klassen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-893">Type reflection support split between <xref:System.Type> and <xref:System.Reflection.TypeInfo> classes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-894">Siehe [Reflektion in .NET Framework für Windows Store-Apps](../../../docs/framework/reflection-and-codedom/reflection-for-windows-store-apps.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-894">See [Reflection in the .NET Framework for Windows Store Apps](../../../docs/framework/reflection-and-codedom/reflection-for-windows-store-apps.md).</span></span>

### <a name="managed-extensibility-framework-mef"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-895">Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-895">Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-896">In [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] bietet das Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF) folgende neue Funktionen:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-896">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], the Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF) provides the following new features:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-897">Unterstützung von generischen Typen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-897">Support for generic types.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-898">Konventionsbasiertes Programmiermodell zum Erstellen von Teilen auf Grundlage von Namenskonventionen anstelle von Attributen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-898">Convention-based programming model that enables you to create parts based on naming conventions rather than attributes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-899">Mehrere Bereiche.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-899">Multiple scopes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-900">Eine Teilmenge von MEF, die Sie verwenden können, wenn Sie Apps im [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] erstellen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-900">A subset of MEF that you can use when you create [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-901">Diese Teilmenge steht als [herunterladbares Paket](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=256238) in der NuGet Gallery zur Verfügung.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-901">This subset is available as a [downloadable package](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=256238) from the NuGet Gallery.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-902">Öffnen Sie zum Installieren des Pakets das Projekt in Visual Studio, wählen Sie im Menü **Projekt** die Option **NuGet-Pakete verwalten** aus, und suchen Sie online nach dem `Microsoft.Composition`-Paket.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-902">To install the package, open your project in Visual Studio, choose **Manage NuGet Packages** from the **Project** menu, and search online for the `Microsoft.Composition` package.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-903">Weitere Informationen finden Sie unter [Übersicht über das Managed Extensibility Framework](../../../docs/framework/mef/index.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-903">For more information, see [Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF)](../../../docs/framework/mef/index.md).</span></span>

### <a name="asynchronous-file-operations"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-904">Asynchrone Dateivorgänge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-904">Asynchronous file operations</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-905">In [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] wurden neue asynchrone Funktionen zu den Programmiersprachen C# und Visual Basic hinzugefügt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-905">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], new asynchronous features were added to the C# and Visual Basic languages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-906">Diese Funktionen ergänzen ein aufgabenbasiertes Modell zum Ausführen von asynchronen Vorgängen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-906">These features add a task-based model for performing asynchronous operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-907">Verwenden Sie dieses neue Modell mithilfe der asynchronen Methoden in den E/A-Klassen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-907">To use this new model, use the asynchronous methods in the I/O classes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-908">Siehe [Asynchrone Datei-E/A](../../../docs/standard/io/asynchronous-file-i-o.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-908">See [Asynchronous File I/O](../../../docs/standard/io/asynchronous-file-i-o.md).</span></span>

<a name="tools"></a> 
### <a name="tools"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-909">Tools</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-909">Tools</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-910">In [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] können Sie mit dem Resource File Generator-Tool (Resgen.exe) aus einer RESOURCES-Datei, die in einer .NET Framework-Assembly eingebettet ist, eine RESW-Datei für [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]-Apps erstellen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-910">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], Resource File Generator (Resgen.exe) enables you to create a .resw file for use in [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps from a .resources file embedded in a .NET Framework assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-911">Weitere Informationen finden Sie unter [Resgen.exe (Resource File Generator)](../../../docs/framework/tools/resgen-exe-resource-file-generator.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-911">For more information, see [Resgen.exe (Resource File Generator)](../../../docs/framework/tools/resgen-exe-resource-file-generator.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-912">Mit Managed Profile Guided Optimization (Mpgo.exe) können Sie die Anwendungsstartzeit, die Arbeitsspeicherauslastung (Workingsetgröße) und den Durchsatz verbessern, indem Sie die Assemblys systemeigener Abbilder optimieren.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-912">Managed Profile Guided Optimization (Mpgo.exe) enables you to improve application startup time, memory utilization (working set size), and throughput by optimizing native image assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-913">Das Befehlszeilentool generiert Profildaten für Anwendungsassemblys systemeigener Abbilder.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-913">The command-line tool generates profile data for native image application assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-914">Siehe [Mpgo.exe (verwaltetes, profilgesteuertes Optimierungstool)](../../../docs/framework/tools/mpgo-exe-managed-profile-guided-optimization-tool.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-914">See [Mpgo.exe (Managed Profile Guided Optimization Tool)](../../../docs/framework/tools/mpgo-exe-managed-profile-guided-optimization-tool.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-915">Ab [!INCLUDE[vs_dev12](../../../includes/vs-dev12-md.md)] können Sie Mpgo.exe verwenden, um [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]-Apps und Desktop-Apps zu optimieren.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-915">Starting with [!INCLUDE[vs_dev12](../../../includes/vs-dev12-md.md)], you can use Mpgo.exe to optimize [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps as well as desktop apps.</span></span>

### <a name="parallel-computing"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-916">Parallele Computervorgänge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-916">Parallel computing</span></span>

<a name="networking"></a> 
### <a name="networking"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-925">Netzwerk</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-925">Networking</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-926">[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] stellt eine neue Programmierschnittstelle für HTTP-Anwendungen bereit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-926">The [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] provides a new programming interface for HTTP applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-927">Weitere Informationen finden Sie in den neuen Namespaces <xref:System.Net.Http?displayProperty=nameWithType> und <xref:System.Net.Http.Headers?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-927">For more information, see the new <xref:System.Net.Http?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Net.Http.Headers?displayProperty=nameWithType> namespaces.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-928">Unterstützt wird jetzt auch eine neue Programmierschnittstelle, um eine WebSocket-Verbindung mithilfe der vorhandenen <xref:System.Net.HttpListener>-Klasse und verknüpften Klassen anzunehmen und mit dieser zu interagieren.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-928">Support is also included for a new programming interface for accepting and interacting with a WebSocket connection by using the existing <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> and related classes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-929">Weitere Informationen finden Sie im neuen <xref:System.Net.WebSockets>-Namespace und in der <xref:System.Net.HttpListener>-Klasse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-929">For more information, see the new <xref:System.Net.WebSockets> namespace and the <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> class.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-930">Darüber hinaus enthält [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] folgende Netzwerkfunktionsverbesserungen:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-930">In addition, the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] includes the following networking improvements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-931">RFC-kompatible URI-Unterstützung.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-931">RFC-compliant URI support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-932">Weitere Informationen finden Sie in der <xref:System.Uri>-Klasse und verknüpften Klassen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-932">For more information, see <xref:System.Uri> and related classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-933">Unterstützung für IDN (Internationalized Domain Name)-Analysen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-933">Support for Internationalized Domain Name (IDN) parsing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-934">Weitere Informationen finden Sie in der <xref:System.Uri>-Klasse und verknüpften Klassen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-934">For more information, see <xref:System.Uri> and related classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-935">Unterstützung für E-Mail-Adressen-Internationalisierung (EAI).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-935">Support for Email Address Internationalization (EAI).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-936">Weitere Informationen finden Sie unter den Ausführungen zum <xref:System.Net.Mail>-Namespace.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-936">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.Mail> namespace.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-937">Verbesserte IPv6-Unterstützung.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-937">Improved IPv6 support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-938">Weitere Informationen finden Sie unter den Ausführungen zum <xref:System.Net.NetworkInformation>-Namespace.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-938">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.NetworkInformation> namespace.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-939">Dual-Modus-Socket-Unterstützung.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-939">Dual-mode socket support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-940">Weitere Informationen finden Sie in den Ausführungen zur <xref:System.Net.Sockets.Socket>-Klasse und zur <xref:System.Net.Sockets.TcpListener>-Klasse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-940">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.Sockets.Socket> and <xref:System.Net.Sockets.TcpListener> classes.</span></span>

### <a name="windows-presentation-foundation-wpf"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-941">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-941">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-942">In der Version [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] wurde Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF) in vielen Bereichen überarbeitet und verbessert. Dazu gehören:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-942">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF) contains changes and improvements in the following areas:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-943">Das neue <xref:System.Windows.Controls.Ribbon.Ribbon>-Steuerelement, mit dem Sie eine Menüband-Benutzeroberfläche implementieren können, die eine Symbolleiste für den Schnellzugriff, ein Anwendungsmenü und Registerkarten hostet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-943">The new <xref:System.Windows.Controls.Ribbon.Ribbon> control, which enables you to implement a ribbon user interface that hosts a Quick Access Toolbar, Application Menu, and tabs.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-944">Die neue <xref:System.ComponentModel.INotifyDataErrorInfo>-Schnittstelle, die synchrone und asynchrone Datenvalidierung unterstützt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-944">The new <xref:System.ComponentModel.INotifyDataErrorInfo> interface, which supports synchronous and asynchronous data validation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-945">Neue Funktionen für die <xref:System.Windows.Controls.VirtualizingPanel>- und <xref:System.Windows.Threading.Dispatcher>-Klassen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-945">New features for the <xref:System.Windows.Controls.VirtualizingPanel> and <xref:System.Windows.Threading.Dispatcher> classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-946">Verbesserte Leistung beim Anzeigen großer Datengruppierungen sowie durch den Zugriff auf Auflistungen in Nicht-UI-Threads.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-946">Improved performance when displaying large sets of grouped data, and by accessing collections on non-UI threads.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-947">Datenbindung an statische Eigenschaften, Datenbindung an benutzerdefinierte Typen, die die <xref:System.Reflection.ICustomTypeProvider>-Schnittstelle implementieren, und Abrufen von Datenbindungsinformationen von einem Bindungsausdruck.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-947">Data binding to static properties, data binding to custom types that implement the <xref:System.Reflection.ICustomTypeProvider> interface, and retrieval of data binding information from a binding expression.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-948">Neupositionierung von Daten bei Wertänderung (Live-Strukturierung).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-948">Repositioning of data as the values change (live shaping).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-949">Überprüfen einer möglicherweise getrennten Verbindung des Datenkontexts für einen Elementcontainer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-949">Ability to check whether the data context for an item container is disconnected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-950">Festlegen der Zeit, die zwischen Eigenschaftenänderungen und Datenquellenupdates verstreichen soll.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-950">Ability to set the amount of time that should elapse between property changes and data source updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-951">Verbesserte Unterstützung für das Implementieren schwacher Ereignismuster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-951">Improved support for implementing weak event patterns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-952">Zudem können Ereignisse jetzt Markuperweiterungen akzeptieren.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-952">Also, events can now accept markup extensions.</span></span>

<a name="windows_communication_foundation"></a> 
### <a name="windows-communication-foundation-wcf"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-953">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-953">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-954">Um das Schreiben und Verwalten von Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)-Anwendungen zu erleichtern, wurden in [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] folgende Funktionen hinzugefügt:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-954">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], the following features have been added to make it simpler to write and maintain Windows Communication Foundation (WCF) applications:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-955">Vereinfachung von generierten Konfigurationsdateien.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-955">Simplification of generated configuration files.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-956">Unterstützung für Contract-First-Entwicklung.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-956">Support for contract-first development.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-957">Leichteres Konfigurieren des ASP.NET-Kompatibilitätsmodus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-957">Ability to configure ASP.NET compatibility mode more easily.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-958">Änderungen in den standardmäßigen Transporteigenschaftswerten, um die Wahrscheinlichkeit zu reduzieren, dass Sie sie festlegen müssen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-958">Changes in default transport property values to reduce the likelihood that you will have to set them.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-959">Updates der <xref:System.Xml.XmlDictionaryReaderQuotas>-Klasse, um die Wahrscheinlichkeit zu reduzieren, dass Sie Kontingente für XML-Wörterbuch-Reader manuell konfigurieren müssen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-959">Updates to the <xref:System.Xml.XmlDictionaryReaderQuotas> class to reduce the likelihood that you will have to manually configure quotas for XML dictionary readers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-960">Validierung von WCF-Konfigurationsdateien von Visual Studio als Teil des Buildprozesses, sodass Sie Konfigurationsfehler erkennen können, bevor Sie die Anwendung ausführen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-960">Validation of WCF configuration files by Visual Studio as part of the build process, so you can detect configuration errors before you run your application.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-961">Neue Unterstützung für asynchrones Streaming.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-961">New asynchronous streaming support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-962">Neue HTTPS-Protokollzuordnung zur leichteren Bereitstellung eines Endpunkts über HTTPS mit IIS (Internetinformationsdienste).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-962">New HTTPS protocol mapping to make it easier to expose an endpoint over HTTPS with Internet Information Services (IIS).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-963">Generieren von Metadaten in einem einzelnen WSDL-Dokument durch Anfügen von `?singleWSDL` an die Dienst-URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-963">Ability to generate metadata in a single WSDL document by appending `?singleWSDL` to the service URL.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-964">Websockets-Unterstützung für echte bidirektionale Kommunikation über die Ports 80 und 443 mit TCP-transportähnlichen Leistungsmerkmalen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-964">Websockets support to enable true bidirectional communication over ports 80 and 443 with performance characteristics similar to the TCP transport.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-965">Unterstützung für das Konfigurieren von Diensten im Code.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-965">Support for configuring services in code.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-966">XML-Editor-QuickInfos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-966">XML Editor tooltips.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-967">Unterstützung von <xref:System.ServiceModel.ChannelFactory>-Cachediensten.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-967"><xref:System.ServiceModel.ChannelFactory> caching support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-968">Unterstützung für die Komprimierung binärer Encoder.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-968">Binary encoder compression support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-969">Unterstützung für einen UDP-Transport, mit dem Entwickler "Fire and Forget" (Auslösen und Vergessen)-Messaging-Dienste schreiben können.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-969">Support for a UDP transport that enables developers to write services that use "fire and forget" messaging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-970">Ein Client sendet eine Nachricht an einen Dienst und erwartet von diesem keine Antwort.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-970">A client sends a message to a service and expects no response from the service.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-971">Unterstützung mehrerer Authentifizierungsmodi auf einem einzelnen WCF-Endpunkt beim Verwenden von HTTP-Transport und -Transportsicherheit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-971">Ability to support multiple authentication modes on a single WCF endpoint when using the HTTP transport and transport security.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-972">Unterstützung für WCF-Dienste, die internationale Domänennamen (IDNs) verwenden.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-972">Support for WCF services that use internationalized domain names (IDNs).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-973">Weitere Informationen finden Sie unter [Neues in Windows Communication Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228173).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-973">For more information, see [What's New in Windows Communication Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228173).</span></span>

<a name="windows_workflow_foundation"></a> 
### <a name="windows-workflow-foundation-wf"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-974">Windows Workflow Foundation (WF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-974">Windows Workflow Foundation (WF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-975">In der Version [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] gibt es jetzt viele neue Funktionen in Windows Workflow Foundation (WF), darunter:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-975">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], several new features were added to Windows Workflow Foundation (WF), including:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-976">Zustandsautomatworkflows, die zunächst als Teil von .NET Framework 4.0.1 ([.NET Framework 4 Platform-Update 1](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=215092)) eingeführt wurden.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-976">State machine workflows, which were first introduced as part of the .NET Framework 4.0.1 ([.NET Framework 4 Platform Update 1](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=215092)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-977">Dieses Update umfasste mehrere neue Klassen und Aktivitäten, sodass Entwickler Zustandsautomatworkflows erstellen konnten.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-977">This update included several new classes and activities that enabled developers to create state machine workflows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-978">Diese Klassen und Aktivitäten wurden für [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] aktualisiert und umfassen nun Folgendes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-978">These classes and activities were updated for the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] to include:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-979">Festlegen von Haltepunkten für Zustände.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-979">The ability to set breakpoints on states.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-980">Kopieren und Einfügen von Übergängen im Workflow Designer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-980">The ability to copy and paste transitions in the workflow designer.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-981">Designerunterstützung für das Erstellen von freigegebenen Triggerübergängen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-981">Designer support for shared trigger transition creation.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-982">Aktivitäten zum Erstellen von Zustandsautomatworkflows, einschließlich <xref:System.Activities.Statements.StateMachine>, <xref:System.Activities.Statements.State> und <xref:System.Activities.Statements.Transition>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-982">Activities for creating state machine workflows, including: <xref:System.Activities.Statements.StateMachine>, <xref:System.Activities.Statements.State>, and <xref:System.Activities.Statements.Transition>.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-983">Verbesserte Workflow Designer-Funktionen, z. B.:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-983">Enhanced Workflow Designer features such as the following:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-984">Verbesserte Workflowsuchfunktionen in Visual Studio, einschließlich **Schnellsuche** und **In Dateien suchen**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-984">Enhanced workflow search capabilities in Visual Studio, including **Quick Find** and **Find in Files**.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-985">Automatisches Erstellen einer Sequenzaktivität, wenn eine zweite untergeordnete Aktivität zu einer Containeraktivität hinzugefügt wird, und Einschließen beider Aktivitäten in die Sequenzaktivität.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-985">Ability to automatically create a Sequence activity when a second child activity is added to a container activity, and to include both activities in the Sequence activity.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-986">Schwenk-Unterstützung zur Änderung des sichtbaren Teils eines Workflows ohne die Verwendung von Bildlaufleisten.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-986">Panning support, which enables the visible portion of a workflow to be changed without using the scroll bars.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-987">Die neue Ansicht **Dokumentgliederung**, die die Gliederungsansicht der Workflowkomponenten in einer Baumstruktur anzeigt und die Auswahl einer Komponente in der Ansicht **Dokumentgliederung** ermöglicht.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-987">A new **Document Outline** view that shows the components of a workflow in a tree-style outline view and lets you select a component in the **Document Outline** view.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-988">Hinzufügen von Anmerkungen zu Aktivitäten.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-988">Ability to add annotations to activities.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-989">Definieren und Verarbeiten von Aktivitätsdelegaten mit dem Workflow Designer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-989">Ability to define and consume activity delegates by using the workflow designer.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-990">Automatisches Verbinden und Einfügen für Aktivitäten und Übergänge in Zustandsautomaten- und Flussdiagrammworkflows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-990">Auto-connect and auto-insert for activities and transitions in state machine and flowchart workflows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-991">Speichern der Ansichtszustandsinformationen für einen Workflow in einem einzelnen Element in der XAML-Datei, sodass Sie die Ansichtszustandsinformationen leicht finden und bearbeiten können.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-991">Storage of the view state information for a workflow in a single element in the XAML file, so you can easily locate and edit the view state information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-992">Eine NoPersistScope-Containeraktivität, damit untergeordnete Aktivitäten nicht beibehalten werden.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-992">A NoPersistScope container activity to prevent child activities from persisting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-993">Unterstützung von C#-Ausdrücken:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-993">Support for C# expressions:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-994">Visual Basic-Workflowprojekte verwenden Visual Basic-Ausdrücke, und C#-Workflowprojekte verwenden C#-Ausdrücke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-994">Workflow projects that use Visual Basic will use Visual Basic expressions, and C# workflow projects will use C# expressions.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-995">C#-Workflowprojekte, die in Visual Studio 2010 erstellt wurden und Visual Basic-Ausdrücke verwenden, sind mit C#-Workflowprojekten, die C#-Ausdrücke verwenden, kompatibel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-995">C# workflow projects that were created in Visual Studio 2010 and that have Visual Basic expressions are compatible with C# workflow projects that use C# expressions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-996">Versionsverwaltungserweiterungen:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-996">Versioning enhancements:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-997">Die neue <xref:System.Activities.WorkflowIdentity>-Klasse, die eine Zuordnung zwischen einer beibehaltenen Workflowinstanz und ihrer Workflowdefinition bietet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-997">The new  <xref:System.Activities.WorkflowIdentity> class, which provides a mapping between a persisted workflow instance and its workflow definition.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-998">Parallele Ausführung mehrerer Workflowversionen im selben Host, einschließlich <xref:System.ServiceModel.Activities.WorkflowServiceHost>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-998">Side-by-side execution of multiple workflow versions in the same host, including <xref:System.ServiceModel.Activities.WorkflowServiceHost>.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-999">Die Änderbarkeit der Definition einer beibehaltenen Workflowinstanz im Rahmen eines dynamischen Updates.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-999">In Dynamic Update, the ability to modify the definition of a persisted workflow instance.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1000">Contract-First-Workflowdienstentwicklung, die das automatische Generieren von Aktivitäten zur Übereinstimmung mit einem vorhandenen Dienstvertrag unterstützt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1000">Contract-first workflow service development, which provides support for automatically generating activities to match an existing service contract.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1001">Weitere Informationen finden Sie unter [Neues in Windows Workflow Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228176).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1001">For more information, see [What's New in Windows Workflow Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228176).</span></span>

<a name="tailored"></a> 
### [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]
 [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1002">-Apps werden für bestimmte Formularfaktoren entworfen und nutzen die Leistungsfähigkeit des Windows-Betriebssystems.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1002"> apps are designed for specific form factors and leverage the power of the Windows operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1003">Eine Teilmenge von [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] oder 4.5.1 kann mithilfe von C# oder Visual Basic zum Erstellen von [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]-Apps in Windows verwendet werden.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1003">A subset of the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] or 4.5.1 is available for building [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps for Windows by using C# or Visual Basic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1004">Diese Teilmenge wird [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)] genannt und in einer [Übersicht](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228491) im Windows Developer Center erläutert.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1004">This subset is called [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)] and is discussed in an [overview](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228491) in the Windows Dev Center.</span></span>

<a name="portable"></a> 
### <a name="portable-class-libraries"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1005">Portable Klassenbibliotheken</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1005">Portable Class Libraries</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1006">Mit dem Projekt "Portable Klassenbibliothek" in [!INCLUDE[vs_dev11_long](../../../includes/vs-dev11-long-md.md)] (und Folgeversionen) können Sie verwaltete Assemblys, die auf mehreren .NET Framework-Plattformen ausgeführt werden können, schreiben und erstellen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1006">The Portable Class Library project in [!INCLUDE[vs_dev11_long](../../../includes/vs-dev11-long-md.md)] (and later versions) enables you to write and build managed assemblies that work on multiple .NET Framework platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1007">Mit einem "Portable Klassenbibliothek"-Projekt wählen Sie die Zielplattformen (wie Windows Phone und [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1007">Using a Portable Class Library project, you choose the platforms (such as Windows Phone and [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]) to target.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1008">Die verfügbaren Typen und Member im Projekt werden automatisch auf die allgemeinen Typen und Member dieser Plattformen beschränkt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1008">The available types and members in your project are automatically restricted to the common types and members across these platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2c7a6-1009">Weitere Informationen finden Sie in der Dokumentation zur [Portablen Klassenbibliothek](../../../docs/standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c7a6-1009">For more information, see [Portable Class Library](../../../docs/standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md).</span></span>
